###############################################################################
### Customization #############################################################
###############################################################################

#This filter contains toggles that can be used to change the behavior of
#the script. It will however work just fine in its default state and is
#actually used in that state by the author.

#Please be aware that you will need Filtration (recommended) or an editor
#that is capable of replacing all occurances of a search token (Replace All).

#Filtration can be found at https://www.pathofexile.com/forum/view-thread/1287447/


# Example usage:
#Let's assume you're playing a 2 hand marauder that primarily uses strength
#items and isn't interested in pure dex/int armour, 1 hand weapons, staffs and bows.
#
#First, let's hide every piece of gear that is tagged as "Progression":
# 1. Replace "Show	#Gear - Progression" by "Hide	#Gear - Progression"
#
#Now let's enable the gear we're actually interested in:
# 2. Replace "Hide	#Gear - Progression - Armour - STR" by		"Show	#Gear - Progression - Armour - STR"
# 3. Replace "Hide	#Gear - Progression - Armour - STR/INT"	by	"Show	#Gear - Progression - Armour - STR/INT"
# 4. Replace "Hide	#Gear - Progression - Armour - DEX/STR" by	"Show	#Gear - Progression - Armour - DEX/STR"
# 5. Replace "Hide	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Two Hand" by	"Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Two Hand"
#
#This will show STR and STR hybrid armour as well as Two Hand Maces/Swords/Axes.
#The usual highlighting for top tier items based on zonelevel will still apply.
#In addition top tier rares of other bases will be shown as well.


#Similiar toggles are available for endgame (T1 + Craft Bases) items. Due to the amount of toggles available
#it is highly recommended to use Filtration if you wish to modify that area.




#The list below is a subsection of available toggles.
#There are more throughout the script, however I do not recommend
#using them unless you are sure what you are doing.

#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - One Hand Axes - Lowlevel
#	Hide	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - One Hand Axes - No Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - One Hand Axes - 3/4 Linked Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - One Hand Axes - 3/4 Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - One Hand Swords - Lowlevel
#	Hide	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - One Hand Swords - No Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - One Hand Swords - 3/4 Linked Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - One Hand Swords - 3/4 Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Two Hand Maces - Lowlevel
#	Hide	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Two Hand Maces - No Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Two Hand Maces - 3/4 Linked Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Two Hand Maces - 3/4 Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Bows - Lowlevel
#	Hide	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Bows - No Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Bows - 3/4 Linked Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Bows - 3/4 Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Thrusting One Hand Swords - Lowlevel
#	Hide	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Thrusting One Hand Swords - No Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Thrusting One Hand Swords - 3/4 Linked Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Thrusting One Hand Swords - 3/4 Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Daggers - Lowlevel
#	Hide	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Daggers - No Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Daggers - 3/4 Linked Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Daggers - 3/4 Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - One Hand Maces - Lowlevel
#	Hide	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - One Hand Maces - No Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - One Hand Maces - 3/4 Linked Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - One Hand Maces - 3/4 Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Two Hand Axes - Lowlevel
#	Hide	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Two Hand Axes - No Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Two Hand Axes - 3/4 Linked Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Two Hand Axes - 3/4 Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Two Hand Swords - Lowlevel
#	Hide	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Two Hand Swords - No Sockets
#	Show	#Gear - Progression - Weapon - Two Hand Swords - 3/4 Linked Sockets

###############################################################################
# Section: ### Specials #######################################################
###############################################################################

#Fishing Rod
Show
	BaseType "Fishing Rod"
	SetTextColor 0 255 150		#Fishing Rod
	SetBorderColor 0 255 150	#Fishing Rod
	SetFontSize 45
	PlayAlertSound 5 300

#Hideout Doodads & Microtransactions
Show
	Class "Hideout Doodads" "Microtransactions"

#Quest Items
Show
	Class "Quest"

#Tabula Rasa Exception, show it as a regular unique
Show
	BaseType "Simple Robe"
	Rarity Unique
	SocketGroup WWWWWW
	
#6L
Show
	LinkedSockets 6
	SetTextColor 0 255 150		#6L
	SetBorderColor 0 255 150	#6L
	SetFontSize 45
	PlayAlertSound 5 300

#5L
Show
	LinkedSockets 5
	Class "Body Armours"
	SetBorderColor 0 255 150	#5L
	SetFontSize 40
	PlayAlertSound 1 175
Show
	LinkedSockets 5
	Class "Bows"
	ItemLevel >= 64
	SetBorderColor 0 255 150	#5L
	SetFontSize 40
	PlayAlertSound 1 175
Show
	LinkedSockets 5
	Class "Staves"
	ItemLevel >= 55
	SetBorderColor 0 255 150	#5L
	SetFontSize 40
	PlayAlertSound 1 175
Show
	LinkedSockets 5
	SetBorderColor 0 255 150	#5L

#6s
Show
	Sockets 6
	SetBorderColor 0 255 150	#6s

#Sacrificial Garb
Show
	BaseType "Sacrificial Garb"
	SetBorderColor 127 127 127	#Sacrificial Garb

# Section: ### Gems ###########################################################
###############################################################################

#Gems - Q10+
Show	#Gems - ~Q10+
	Class "Gems"
	Quality >= 10
	SetBorderColor 27 162 155	#Gems - Q10+
	SetTextColor 27 162 155		#Gems - Q10+
	SetBackgroundColor 0 0 0 255	#Gems - Q10+
#Gems - Q1+
Show	#Gems - ~Q1+
	Class "Gems"
	Quality >= 1
	SetBorderColor 27 162 155 0	#Gems - Q1+
	SetTextColor 27 162 155		#Gems - Q1+
	SetBackgroundColor 0 0 0 255	#Gems - Q1+
#Gems - DropOnly
Show	#Gems - ~DropOnly
	Class "Gems"
	BaseType "Portal" "Detonate Mines" "Empower" "Enhance" "Enlighten" "Added Chaos Damage"
	SetTextColor 27 162 155		#Gems - DropOnly
	SetBackgroundColor 0 0 0 255	#Gems - DropOnly
#Gems - Vaal
Show	#Gems - ~Vaal
	Class "Gems"
	BaseType "Vaal"
	SetTextColor 27 162 155		#Gems - Vaal
#Gems - Active
Show	#Gems - Active
	Class "Active Skill Gems"
	SetTextColor 27 162 155		#Gems - Active
	SetFontSize 28
#Gems - Support
Show	#Gems - Support
	Class "Support Skill Gems"
	SetTextColor 27 162 155		#Gems - Support
	SetFontSize 28
#Gems - CatchAll
Show	#Gems - ~CatchAll
	Class "Gems"
	SetTextColor 27 162 155		#Gems - CatchAll
	SetFontSize 28

# Section: ### Maps ###########################################################

#Maps - DropLevel 79+
Show
	Class "Maps"
	DropLevel >= 79
	SetBorderColor 150 0 0		#Maps 79+
	SetFontSize 45
	PlayAlertSound 6 250

#Maps - DropLevel <= 73 (Good Bases)
Show	#~Maps - DropLevel <= 73 (Good Bases)
	Class "Maps"
	DropLevel <= 73
	BaseType "Tropical Island Map" "Mountain Ledge Map" "Underground Sea Map" "Strand" "Dry Woods Map" "Pier Map" "Wharf" "Promenade Map" "Shore Map"
	SetBackgroundColor 0 0 0 255	#Maps - DropLevel <= 73 (Good Bases)

#Maps - DropLevel <= 73
Show	#~Maps - DropLevel <= 73
	Class "Maps"
	DropLevel <= 73

#Maps - DropLevel 74 - 78 (Good Bases)
Show	#Maps - DropLevel 74 - 78 (Good Bases)
	Class "Maps"
	BaseType "Canyon Map" "Arid Lake Map" "Gorge Map" "Plateau Map" "Dry Peninsula Map"
	PlayAlertSound 2 200
	SetFontSize 38
	SetBackgroundColor 0 0 0 255	#Maps - DropLevel 74 - 78 (Good Bases)

#Maps - CatchAll
Show	#~Maps - CatchAll
	Class "Maps"
	PlayAlertSound 2 200
	SetFontSize 38

#Maps - Fragments
Show	#~Maps - Fragments
	Class "Map Fragments"
